(function(){

        if (typeof(_spBodyOnLoadFunctions) === 'undefined' || _spBodyOnLoadFunctions === null) {
            return;
        }
        _spBodyOnLoadFunctions.push(function() 
        {
          ExecuteOrDelayUntilScriptLoaded(
            function()
            {
              var pairs = SP.ScriptHelpers.getDocumentQueryPairs();
              var followDoc, itemId, listId, docName;
              for (var key in pairs)
              {
                if(key.toLowerCase() == 'followdocument') 
                  followDoc = pairs[key];
                else if(key.toLowerCase() == 'itemid') 
                  itemId = pairs[key];
                else if(key.toLowerCase() == 'listid') 
                  listId = pairs[key];
                else if(key.toLowerCase() == 'docname') 
                  docName = decodeURI(pairs[key]);
              } 

              if(followDoc != null && followDoc == '1' && listId!=null && itemId != null && docName != null)
              {
                SP.SOD.executeFunc('followingcommon.js', 'FollowDocumentFromEmail', function() 
                { 
                  FollowDocumentFromEmail(itemId, listId, docName);
                });
              }

            }, 'SP.init.js');

        });
    })();(function(){

        if (typeof(_spBodyOnLoadFunctions) === 'undefined' || _spBodyOnLoadFunctions === null) {
            return;
        }
        _spBodyOnLoadFunctions.push(function() {

            if (typeof(SPClientTemplates) === 'undefined' || SPClientTemplates === null || (typeof(APD_InAssetPicker) === 'function' && APD_InAssetPicker())) {
                return;
            }

            var renderFollowFooter = function(renderCtx,  calloutActionMenu)
            {
                if (renderCtx.ListTemplateType == 700) 
                    myDocsActionsMenuPopulator(renderCtx, calloutActionMenu);
                else
                    CalloutOnPostRenderTemplate(renderCtx, calloutActionMenu);

                var listItem = renderCtx.CurrentItem;
                if (typeof(listItem) === 'undefined' || listItem === null) {
                    return;
                }
                if (listItem.FSObjType == 0) {
                    calloutActionMenu.addAction(new CalloutAction({
                        text: Strings.STS.L_CalloutFollowAction,
                        tooltip: Strings.STS.L_CalloutFollowAction_Tooltip,
                        onClickCallback: function (calloutActionClickEvent, calloutAction) {
                            var callout = GetCalloutFromRenderCtx(renderCtx);
                            if (!(typeof(callout) === 'undefined' || callout === null))
                                callout.close();
                            SP.SOD.executeFunc('followingcommon.js', 'FollowSelectedDocument', function() { FollowSelectedDocument(renderCtx); });
                        }
                    }));
                }
            };

            var registerOverride = function(id) {
                var followingOverridePostRenderCtx = {};
                followingOverridePostRenderCtx.BaseViewID = 'Callout';
                followingOverridePostRenderCtx.ListTemplateType = id;
                followingOverridePostRenderCtx.Templates = {};
                followingOverridePostRenderCtx.Templates.Footer = function(renderCtx) {
                    var  renderECB;
                    if (typeof(isSharedWithMeView) === 'undefined' || isSharedWithMeView === null) {
                        renderECB = true;
                    } else {
                        var viewCtx = getViewCtxFromCalloutCtx(renderCtx);
                        renderECB = !isSharedWithMeView(viewCtx);
                    }
                    return CalloutRenderFooterTemplate(renderCtx, renderFollowFooter, renderECB);
                };
                SPClientTemplates.TemplateManager.RegisterTemplateOverrides(followingOverridePostRenderCtx);
            }
            registerOverride(101);
            registerOverride(700);
        });

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function MSOLayout_GetRealOffset(StartingObject, OffsetType, EndParent) {
                    var realValue = 0;
                    if (!EndParent) EndParent = document.body;
                    for (var currentObject = StartingObject; currentObject && currentObject != EndParent && currentObject != document.body; currentObject = currentObject.offsetParent) {
                        var offset = eval('currentObject.offset' + OffsetType);
                        if (offset) realValue += offset;
                    }
                    return realValue;
                }

                //this function adds the necessary property to HTMLDivElement so the Infragistics menus work
                $(document).ready(function () {
                    if (typeof HTMLDivElement != "undefined") {
                        if (typeof HTMLDivElement.prototype.runtimeStyle == "undefined") {
                            HTMLDivElement.prototype.runtimeStyle = function () { this.filter = ""; }
                        }
                    }
                });
   </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function AccountClick() {
           jQuery('ul.button-account').toggleClass('open');

           var isVisible = jQuery('ul.button-settings').is(':visible');
           if (isVisible) {
               jQuery('ul.button-settings').toggleClass('open');
           }
       }

       function SettingsClick() {
           jQuery('ul.button-settings').toggleClass('open');

           var isVisible = jQuery('ul.button-account').is(':visible');
           if (isVisible) {
               jQuery('ul.button-account').toggleClass('open');
           }
       }

       $('body').on("mouseup touchstart", function (e) {
           var container = jQuery('.button-container');
           var isVisible = jQuery('ul.button-settings').is(':visible');
           if (!container.is(e.target) // if the target of the click isn't the container...
           && container.has(e.target).length === 0 && isVisible) // ... nor a descendant of the container
           {
               jQuery('ul.button-settings').toggleClass('open');
           }
       });

       $('body').on("mouseup touchstart", function (e) {
           var container = jQuery('.button-container');
           var isVisible = jQuery('ul.button-account').is(':visible');
           if (!container.is(e.target) // if the target of the click isn't the container...
           && container.has(e.target).length === 0 && isVisible) // ... nor a descendant of the container
           {
               jQuery('ul.button-account').toggleClass('open');
           }
       });
       </script>

       <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
        function alerts_ShowUnSubscribeeTOCPopup(title, alertType,journalId) {
        var UnSubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
        var lblUnsubscribeMessage = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_lblUnsubscribeMessage');
        lblUnsubscribeMessage.innerHTML = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnSubscribeAlertType').value = alertType;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeMessage').value = title;

        if (document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value == null || document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value == '') {
            document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value = journalId;
        }

        if (UnSubscribeeTOCPopup != null) {
            UnSubscribeeTOCPopup.show();
        }
    }

    function alerts_ShowUnSubscribeeTOCPopup_Root(title, journalId, alertType) {
        var UnSubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
        var lblUnsubscribeMessage = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_lblUnsubscribeMessage');
        lblUnsubscribeMessage.innerHTML = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeMessage').value = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnSubscribeAlertType').value = alertType;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeJournalId').value = journalId;
        if (UnSubscribeeTOCPopup != null) {
            UnSubscribeeTOCPopup.show();
        }
    }
    function alerts_ShowUnSubscribeeTOCPopup_Citation(title, journalId, ovidId) {
        var UnSubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
        var lblUnsubscribeMessage = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_lblUnsubscribeMessage');
        lblUnsubscribeMessage.innerHTML = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeMessage').value = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnSubscribeAlertType').value = 'Citation';
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeJournalId').value = journalId;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenOvidId').value = ovidId;
        if (UnSubscribeeTOCPopup != null) {
            UnSubscribeeTOCPopup.show();
        }

    }

    function alerts_ShowUnSubscribeeTOCPopup_Topical(title, journalId, topicalCollectionId) {
        var UnSubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
        var lblUnsubscribeMessage = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_lblUnsubscribeMessage');
        lblUnsubscribeMessage.innerHTML = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeMessage').value = title;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnSubscribeAlertType').value = 'Topical';
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeJournalId').value = journalId;
        document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenTopicalCollectionId').value = topicalCollectionId;
        
        if (document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value == null || document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value == '') {
            document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value = journalId;
        }
        if (UnSubscribeeTOCPopup != null) {
            UnSubscribeeTOCPopup.show();
        }

    }
  
    function alerts_ShowUnSubscribeeTOCSuccessPopup() {
        var UnSubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
        if (UnSubscribeeTOCPopup != null) {
            UnSubscribeeTOCPopup.show();
        }
    }

    function alerts_CloseUnSubscribeeTOCPopup() {
        var UnSubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
        if (UnSubscribeeTOCPopup != null) {
            UnSubscribeeTOCPopup.hide();
            window.location.href = window.location.href;
        }
    }

       <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
        function alerts_ShowSubscribeeTOCPopup(journalTitle , journalId) 
    {
        var modelPopupState = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenSubscribeToEtocPopupState');
        var emailTextBox = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_txtEmailAddress');
        var thanksPanle = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_pnlAuthenticatedUser');
        var mainPanle = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_pnlMain');
        var thankYouMessageUnAuthenticated = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_lblThankYouMessage');
        var thankYouMessageAuthenticated = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_lblAuthenticatedUserTitle');
        
        if (modelPopupState.value == 'showthanksmessage') 
        {
            thanksPanle.style.display = "block";
            mainPanle.style.display = "none";
            thankYouMessageAuthenticated.innerHTML = "Thank you for subscribing to the eTOC for " + journalTitle;
        }
        
        if (modelPopupState.value == 'showemail') 
        {
            thanksPanle.style.display = "none";
            mainPanle.style.display = "block";
            thankYouMessageUnAuthenticated.innerHTML = "Thank you for choosing to subscribe to the eTOC for " + journalTitle;
        }

        var SubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('subscribeToEtoc');
        
        if (SubscribeeTOCPopup != null) 
        {
            SubscribeeTOCPopup.show();
            document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenJournalId').value = journalId;

            if (modelPopupState.value == 'showemail') 
            {
                emailTextBox.focus();
            }
        }
    }

    function alerts_CloseSubscribeeTOCPopup() 
    {
        var modelPopupState = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenSubscribeToEtocPopupState');
        var pageUrl = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenConfirmSubscriptionPageUrl');
        var SubscribeeTOCPopup = $find('subscribeToEtoc');

        if (SubscribeeTOCPopup != null) 
        {
            SubscribeeTOCPopup.hide();
            if (pageUrl.value != '') 
            {
                window.location = pageUrl.value;

            }
        }
    }
       </script>

                <div allowdelete="false" class="ms-WPBody noindex " haspers="false" id="WebPartWPQ2" style="display:none;" webpartid="f891799c-959e-482f-8de1-84335bfebef8" width="100%">
                 <div id="ctl00_ctl39_g_f891799c_959e_482f_8de1_84335bfebef8">
                  <div id="ej-box-01">
                   <div id="ej-box-01-title">
                    National Nurses Week 2016
                   </div>
                   <div id="ej-box-01-body">
                    <p style="text-align:center;">
                     <img alt="" src="/cinjournal/PublishingImages/NursesWeek16-400x209.jpg" style="margin:5px;"/>
                    </p>
                    <p style="text-align:center;">
                     <font class="ms-rteFontFace-1" style="font-size:9pt;">
                      In honor ofNurses Week, enjoy the current issue of
                      <em>
                       CIN:
                      </em>
                      <em>
                       Computers, Informatics, Nursing
                      </em>
                      for free!
                      <br/>
                      Plus, we will continue celebrating nurses all month long, because a week is just not enough.
                     </font>
                    </p>
                    <p style="text-align:center;">
                     <span class="ms-rteFontFace-1" style="font-size:9pt;">
                      To say thanks for all that you do, we are offering additional free content, special discount offers and more, in conjunction with our partners at
                      <a href="http://www.wolterskluwernursesweek.com/">
                       Wolters Kluwer
                      </a>
                      and
                      <a href="http://www.nursingcenter.com/national-nurses-week">
                       NursingCenter.com
                      </a>
                      .
                     </span>
                    </p>
                    <p style="text-align:center;">
                     <span class="ms-rteFontFace-1" style="font-size:9pt;">
                      Be sure to join the conversations on Social Media by using the hashtags below:
                      <br/>
                      #NursesWeek
                      <br/>
                      #WKnursesweek
                      <br/>
                      #SafeNursesRock
                     </span>
                    </p>
                    <div style="text-align:center;">

              <div class="s4-wpcell-plain ms-webpartzone-cell ms-webpart-cell-vertical ms-fullWidth " id="MSOZoneCell_WebPartWPQ16">
               <div class="ms-webpart-chrome ms-webpart-chrome-vertical ms-webpart-chrome-fullWidth ">
                <div allowdelete="false" class="ms-WPBody noindex " haspers="false" id="WebPartWPQ16" style="" webpartid="93a5f84d-8d3b-470f-93b7-c968d8ed670d" width="100%">
                 <div id="ctl00_ctl39_g_93a5f84d_8d3b_470f_93b7_c968d8ed670d">
                  <div id="ej-box-01">
                   <div id="ej-box-01-title">
                    Call for Papers Announcement
                   </div>
                   <div id="ej-box-01-body">
                    <p style="text-decoration:underline;">
                     <font class="ms-rteFontSize-3" face="Verdana" style="text-decoration:underline;">
                      <font face="Verdana">
                       <strong>
                        Now Accepting Submissions for CIN Plus!
                       </strong>
                      </font>
                     </font>
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     CIN features innovations, emerging technologies, and professional perspectives related to technology in nursing practice, education and research. Interprofessional topics and non-nurse authors are welcome. Tutorials are permitted. CIN Plus articles are shorter in length than regular CIN submissions (2500-3000 words or 10-12 pages double spaced). Instead of an abstract and keywords, CIN Plus articles include three key points that summarize the information conveyed by the article. CIN Plus is an online only feature, published monthly, and can accept charts and images in color. Supplemental material may be published online at no cost to the author.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                      Publishing format: included in the journal of record, indexed in pubmed, available through ovid, published online
                     <br/>
                      Peer-reviewed
                     <br/>
                      Word count: 2500-3000
                     <br/>
                      Structured abstract: none (in lieu of abstract, please include 3-5 bulleted key points)
                     <br/>
                      Tables: up to 2
                     <br/>
                      Figures: up to 5, color acceptable
                     <br/>
                      References: Should be included as appropriate
                     <br/>
                      Supplemental content: Supplemental material including images, slides, and video can be published online at no cost to authors
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Manuscripts should be submitted through CINs online editorial manager system, the
                     <a href="/cinjournal/Pages/instructionsforauthors.aspx">
                      submission link and general author instructions are found here
                     </a>
                     . Make certain to indicate in the cover letter that the submission is intended for CIN Plus.
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

               </div>

                  <script type="text/javascript">
                   var atmcDescription;
var atmcCollectionName;
var atmcRdoExistingCollection;
var atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
var atmcRdoNewCollection;
function atmcGetPopup() { return $find('addToMyCollectionsPopupExtender_1360726500'); }
var atmcPnlMain;
var atmcPnlMessage;
var atmcCmbExistingCollection;
var atmcParaCollectionName;
var atmcParaCollectionDescription;
var atmcCustomValidator;

$(document).ready(function()
	{
		atmc_InitializeControls();
	}	);

function atmc_attachFocusHandler() 
{
    if (atmcPnlMain != null && atmcPnlMain.style.display != 'none' && atmcGetPopup() != null)
    {
        atmcGetPopup().add_shown(atmc_SetFocusOnControl); 
    }
}

function atmc_InitializeControls()
{
    atmcDescription = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_txtDescription');
    atmcCollectionName = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_txtCollectionName');
    atmcRdoExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_rdoExistingCollection');
    atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked = false;
    atmcRdoNewCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_rdoNewCollection');
    atmcPnlMain = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_pnlMain');
    atmcPnlMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_pnlMessage');
    atmcCmbExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_cmbExistingCollection');
    atmcParaCollectionName = $get('paraCollectionName');
    atmcParaCollectionDescription = $get('paraCollectionDescription');
    atmcCustomValidator = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl00_customValidator');
} 

function atmc_SetFocusOnControl() {

    if (atmcCustomValidator != null && atmcCustomValidator.style.display != 'none') {
     
        atmcRdoNewCollection.checked = true;
        atmcCollectionName.disabled = false;
        atmcDescription.disabled = false;
        atmcParaCollectionName.className = "";
        atmcParaCollectionDescription.className = "";
        atmcCmbExistingCollection.disabled = true;
        atmcCollectionName.focus();
        atmcCollectionName.select();
    }
    atmcSetFocus();
}

Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_attachFocusHandler);
//Document.Ready() does not work after postback.This is a problem with partial postback.
//The DOM isn't reloaded and so the document ready function won't be hit again. In order 
//to achieve such functionality we need to assign a partial postback handler.
Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_InitializeControls);

                  <script type="text/javascript">
                   var yourName;
    var emailMessage;
    var colleagueEmail;
    var yourEmail;
    var hiddenEmailToColleague;
    var pnlMainEmail;
    var divErrorMessage;
    var lblErrorMessage;
    var pnlErrorMessage;
    var pnlSuccessMessageEmail;
    var btnSend;
    var chkSendMeCopy;
    var hiddenIsUser;

    $(document).ready(function () {
        emailToColleague_pageLoad();
    });

    function getEmailPopup() { return $find('emailToColleaguePopupExtender__276405444'); }

    function emailToColleague_pageLoad() {

        yourName = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_txtYourName');
        emailMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_txtMessage');
        colleagueEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_txtColleaguesEmail');
        yourEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_txtYourEmail');
        hiddenEmailToColleague = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_hiddenEmailToColleague');
        pnlMainEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_pnlMain');
        divErrorMessage = $get('divErrorMessage')
        lblErrorMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_lblErrorMessage');
        pnlErrorMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_pnlErrorMessage');
        pnlSuccessMessageEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_pnlSuccessMessage');
        btnSend = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_btnSend');
        chkSendMeCopy = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_chkSendMeCopy');
        hiddenIsUser = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_40af8700_835b_41d5_a0ae_a05a577493f4_ctl01_hiddenIsUser');

        if (getEmailPopup() != null) {
            getEmailPopup().add_shown(SetFocus);
        }
    }

    function SetFocus() {
        if (pnlMainEmail.style.display != 'none')
            yourName.focus();
    }

    Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(emailToColleague_pageLoad);

                  <script type="text/javascript">
                   var atmcDescription;
var atmcCollectionName;
var atmcRdoExistingCollection;
var atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
var atmcRdoNewCollection;
function atmcGetPopup() { return $find('addToMyCollectionsPopupExtender_750382944'); }
var atmcPnlMain;
var atmcPnlMessage;
var atmcCmbExistingCollection;
var atmcParaCollectionName;
var atmcParaCollectionDescription;
var atmcCustomValidator;

$(document).ready(function()
	{
		atmc_InitializeControls();
	}	);

function atmc_attachFocusHandler() 
{
    if (atmcPnlMain != null && atmcPnlMain.style.display != 'none' && atmcGetPopup() != null)
    {
        atmcGetPopup().add_shown(atmc_SetFocusOnControl); 
    }
}

function atmc_InitializeControls()
{
    atmcDescription = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_txtDescription');
    atmcCollectionName = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_txtCollectionName');
    atmcRdoExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_rdoExistingCollection');
    atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked = false;
    atmcRdoNewCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_rdoNewCollection');
    atmcPnlMain = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_pnlMain');
    atmcPnlMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_pnlMessage');
    atmcCmbExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_cmbExistingCollection');
    atmcParaCollectionName = $get('paraCollectionName');
    atmcParaCollectionDescription = $get('paraCollectionDescription');
    atmcCustomValidator = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl00_customValidator');
} 

function atmc_SetFocusOnControl() {

    if (atmcCustomValidator != null && atmcCustomValidator.style.display != 'none') {
     
        atmcRdoNewCollection.checked = true;
        atmcCollectionName.disabled = false;
        atmcDescription.disabled = false;
        atmcParaCollectionName.className = "";
        atmcParaCollectionDescription.className = "";
        atmcCmbExistingCollection.disabled = true;
        atmcCollectionName.focus();
        atmcCollectionName.select();
    }
    atmcSetFocus();
}

Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_attachFocusHandler);
//Document.Ready() does not work after postback.This is a problem with partial postback.
//The DOM isn't reloaded and so the document ready function won't be hit again. In order 
//to achieve such functionality we need to assign a partial postback handler.
Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_InitializeControls);

                  <script type="text/javascript">
                   var yourName;
    var emailMessage;
    var colleagueEmail;
    var yourEmail;
    var hiddenEmailToColleague;
    var pnlMainEmail;
    var divErrorMessage;
    var lblErrorMessage;
    var pnlErrorMessage;
    var pnlSuccessMessageEmail;
    var btnSend;
    var chkSendMeCopy;
    var hiddenIsUser;

    $(document).ready(function () {
        emailToColleague_pageLoad();
    });

    function getEmailPopup() { return $find('emailToColleaguePopupExtender__783024864'); }

    function emailToColleague_pageLoad() {

        yourName = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_txtYourName');
        emailMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_txtMessage');
        colleagueEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_txtColleaguesEmail');
        yourEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_txtYourEmail');
        hiddenEmailToColleague = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_hiddenEmailToColleague');
        pnlMainEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_pnlMain');
        divErrorMessage = $get('divErrorMessage')
        lblErrorMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_lblErrorMessage');
        pnlErrorMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_pnlErrorMessage');
        pnlSuccessMessageEmail = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_pnlSuccessMessage');
        btnSend = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_btnSend');
        chkSendMeCopy = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_chkSendMeCopy');
        hiddenIsUser = $get('ctl00_ctl39_g_1ddf9336_1696_4db6_9bd5_53a325dd6db4_ctl01_hiddenIsUser');

        if (getEmailPopup() != null) {
            getEmailPopup().add_shown(SetFocus);
        }
    }

    function SetFocus() {
        if (pnlMainEmail.style.display != 'none')
            yourName.focus();
    }

    Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(emailToColleague_pageLoad);

}

{
if ($(menuDiv).attr("style").toLowerCase().indexOf('block') > 0) {
$(menuDiv).attr("style", "display:none;");
}
}
}

                  <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
                   function fp_forgotPasswordValidate()
{
    var txtEmail = document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_forgotPassword_txtEmail');
    if(txtEmail.value == '')
    {
        alert('Please enter Email Address');
        txtEmail.focus();
        txtEmail.select();  
        return false;
    }
    
    var hiddenForgotPassword = document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_forgotPassword_hiddenForgotPassword');
    hiddenForgotPassword.value = 'true';
    return true;
}
function fp_closeForgotPasswordPopup()
{ 
    //hide modal popup
    var forgotPasswordPopup = $find('sendMailPanel');
    if(forgotPasswordPopup != null)
    {
        forgotPasswordPopup.hide();
    }    
        
    
    //show main panel
    var pnlForgotPassword = document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_forgotPassword_pnlMain');
    var successMessage= document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_forgotPassword_pnlPasswordSent');
    pnlForgotPassword.style.display ='block';
    successMessage.style.display = 'none'; 
    
    //hide error message
    var cvEmailError = document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_forgotPassword_cvEmailError');
    ValidatorEnable(cvEmailError, false);
    
    //clear text box
    var txtEmail = document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_forgotPassword_txtEmail');
    txtEmail.value = '';
}
function fp_showForgotPasswordPopup() {
    //hide modal popup
    var forgotPasswordPopup = $find('sendMailPanel');
    if (forgotPasswordPopup != null) {
        forgotPasswordPopup.show();
    }
}
                  </script>

                    <p>
                     <strong>
                      What does "Remember me" mean?
                     </strong>
                     <br/>
                     By checking this box, you'll stay logged in until you logout. You'll get easier access to your articles, collections,
            media, and all your other content, even if you close your browser or shut down your
            computer.
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     To protect your most sensitive data and activities (like changing your password),
            we'll ask you to re-enter your password when you access these services.
                    </p>

                     <strong>
                      What if I'm on a computer that I share with others?
                     </strong>
                     <br/>
                     If you're using a public computer or you share this computer with others, we recommend
            that you uncheck the "Remember me" box.

                  <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
                   function kml_showKeepMeLoggedInPopup() 
    {
        var keepMeLoggedInPopup = $find('keepMeLoggedInPanel');
        if (keepMeLoggedInPopup != null) {
            keepMeLoggedInPopup.show();
        }
    }
    function kml_closeKeepMeLoggedInPopup() 
    {
        var keepMeLoggedInPopup = $find('keepMeLoggedInPanel');
        if (keepMeLoggedInPopup != null) 
        {
            keepMeLoggedInPopup.hide();
        }
    }
                  </script>
                  <input id="ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_HiddenEJPLoginControlView" name="ctl00$ctl39$g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f$ctl00$HiddenEJPLoginControlView" type="hidden"/>
                  <input id="ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_HiddenSingleSignOn" name="ctl00$ctl39$g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f$ctl00$HiddenSingleSignOn" type="hidden" value="false"/>
                  <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
                   // This function will hide eJP Login Control and will set hidden field's value to collapse.
function HideEjpLoginControl() {

$(".ej-ejp-login-fields").attr("style","display:none;");
$(".ej-sso-login-lww-ex").attr("style","display:block;");
$(".ej-sso-login-lww-col").attr("style","display:none;");
$("#" + "ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_HiddenEJPLoginControlView").val("Collapse");
}

// This function will show eJP Login Control and will set hidden field's value to expand.
function ShowEjpLoginControl() {

$(".ej-ejp-login-fields").attr("style","display:block;");
$(".ej-sso-login-lww-ex").attr("style","display:none;");
$(".ej-sso-login-lww-col").attr("style","display:block;");
$("#" + "ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_HiddenEJPLoginControlView").val("Expand");
}

$(document).ready(function () {

    // We will decide whether to display or hide eJP login control based on hidden field's ('HiddenEJPLoginControlView') value.
    // When ShowSingleSignOn is disabled from the web part we will not make eJP login control expandable or collapsible.
    var HiddenEJPLoginControlView = $("#" + "ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_HiddenEJPLoginControlView").val();
    var HiddenSingleSignOn = $("#" + "ctl00_ctl39_g_5930c8e0_c94c_409b_b373_9be2bc63cb4f_ctl00_HiddenSingleSignOn").val();
    if (HiddenEJPLoginControlView == "Collapse" && HiddenSingleSignOn!="false") {
        HideEjpLoginControl();
    }
    else if (HiddenSingleSignOn!="false") {
        ShowEjpLoginControl();
    }
});
                  </script>

                         </font>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </p>
                    <p style="text-align:center;">
                     <font class="ms-rteFontFace-1 ms-rteFontSize-1">
                      All of your responses will be kept confidential and only looked in the aggregate. Please be sure to include your name and e-mail address at the end of the survey for a chance to win one of 5 American Express Gift Cards. Your information will only be used for this drawing.
                     </font>
                    </p>
                    <p style="text-align:center;">
                     <font class="ms-rteFontFace-1 ms-rteFontSize-1">
                      Thank you in advance for your time and insight.
                      <br/>
                      <em>
                       CIN: Computers, Informatics, Nursing
                      </em>
                      <br/>
                     </font>
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>

               <div class="ms-webpart-chrome ms-webpart-chrome-vertical ms-webpart-chrome-fullWidth ">
                <div allowdelete="false" class="ms-WPBody noindex " haspers="false" id="WebPartctl00_ctl39_g_3fc158fa_4ae6_4aee_8ef4_d6e14727588f" style="" webpartid="3fc158fa-4ae6-4aee-8ef4-d6e14727588f" width="100%">

              <div class="s4-wpcell-plain ms-webpartzone-cell ms-webpart-cell-vertical ms-fullWidth " id="MSOZoneCell_WebPartWPQ11">
               <div class="ms-webpart-chrome ms-webpart-chrome-vertical ms-webpart-chrome-fullWidth ">
                <div allowdelete="false" class="ms-WPBody noindex " haspers="false" id="WebPartWPQ11" style="display:none;" webpartid="7fd0272a-c744-4b03-8494-c6c135fb9da5" width="100%">
                 <div id="ctl00_ctl39_g_7fd0272a_c744_4b03_8494_c6c135fb9da5">
                  <div id="ej-box-02">
                   <div id="ej-box-02-title">
                    <!--needed for IE 6 -->
                   </div>
                   <div id="ej-box-02-body">
                    <p style="text-decoration:underline;">
                     <strong>
                      ANI Emerging Leaders Survey
                     </strong>
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     As a part of an Alliance for Nursing Informatics (ANI) Emerging Leaders project,we invite you to participate in a survey about nurses' perceptions of health information technology (HIT) tools related to the nurse's role in patient engagement at your facility.
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     Your participation is voluntary and the information collected will be used to provide an understanding of the relationship between health IT, nursing and patient engagement. Your personal survey information will remain confidential. Your job will not be affected by whether or not you choose to participate in this survey.
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     The survey will take approximately 10 minutes and is accessible via the following link:
                     <a href="https://tonicforhealth.com/passage/survey/R-8lfa5RNN-9rPN10syhhw/question" style="text-decoration:underline;">
                      <strong>
                       https://tonicforhealth.com/passage/survey/R-8lfa5RNN-9rPN10syhhw/question
                      </strong>
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     <strong>
                      Deadline for completion has been extended to March 31, 2016.
                     </strong>
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     Thank you in advance for your participation and for contributing to this important body of knowledge to advance nursing's role in patient engagement!
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     For more on the ANI Emerging Leaders Program,
                     <a href="http://www.allianceni.org/EmergingLeader.asp">
                      <strong>
                       click here
                      </strong>
                     </a>
                     .
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var oas_tag = {};

    //Specify the ad update interval
    var bannerUpdateInterval = '0';    

    var bannerRefreshTime = 0;
	
    //Define OAS URL "oasc17.247realmedia.com" 
    oas_tag.url = 'oasc17.247realmedia.com'; 
    
    //Get Interstitial Ad Duration
    var interstitialAdDuration = '0';

    //Define size in format [width, height]
    oas_tag.sizes = function () 
    {
        if($('#oas_Top').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Top", [728, 90]); }
        if($('#oas_Top1').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Top1", [300, 600]); }
        if($('#oas_Right').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Right", [300, 250]); }
        if($('#oas_Right1').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Right1", [160, 600]); }
        if($('#oas_Right2').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Right2", [300, 250]); }
        if($('#oas_Bottom').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Bottom", [728, 90]); }
        if($('#oas_Position1').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Position1", [275, 200]); }
        if($('#oas_Position2').length > 0) { oas_tag.definePos("Position2", [80, 25]); }
    };

    // *************************************************************** //
    // for oas_tag.site_page property follow the below rules
    // Include everything after the "http://journals.lwww.com/" but no query string. Also make sure the string is lower cased.

    // for e.g. if the URL for the page = http://journals.lwww.com/anesthesiology/pages/default.aspx 
    // oas_tag.site_page = "anesthesiology/pages/default.aspx";

    // e.g. 2 if the URL for the page = http://journals.lww.com/anesthesiology/toc/2013/01000
    // oas_tag.site_page = "anesthesiology/toc/2013/01000";

    // e.g. 3 if the URL for the page = http://journals.lww.com/anesthesiology/Pages/collectiondetails.aspx?TopicalCollectionId=4
    // oas_tag.site_page = "/anesthesiology/pages/collectiondetails.aspx"; // No QUERY STRING

    // e.g. 4 if the URL for the page = http://journals.lww.com/anesthesiology/Pages/collectiondetails.aspx?TopicalCollectionId=4
    // oas_tag.site_page = "/anesthesiology/pages/collectiondetails.aspx"; // No QUERY STRING

    // Another journal
    // for e.g. if the URL for the page = http://journals.lwww.com/hcmrjournal/pages/default.aspx 
    // oas_tag.site_page = "hcmrjournal/pages/default.aspx";
    // *************************************************************** //
    
    //Defines OAS Site page
    var sitePage = document.location.pathname;	
    if(sitePage != undefined && sitePage != null)
    {		
        oas_tag.site_page = sitePage.substring(1).toLowerCase();
    }
    else
    {		
        oas_tag.site_page = '';
    }
    oas_tag.lazyload = true; //Lazy Load Parameter
    //Define Keywords
    if(window.location && window.location.search && window.location.search.length > 1)
    {
        oas_tag.query = window.location.search.substring(1);
    }
    else
    {
        oas_tag.query = '';
    }

    //***************************************************************//
    // Keep analytics to "true" always.
    // *************************************************************** //
    oas_tag.analytics = true; // required to collect taxonomy & referral data

    //***************************************************************//
    // We are not using taxomomy but leave it in there for future usage.
    // *************************************************************** //
    oas_tag.taxonomy = ''; // taxonomy collection

    oas_tag.allowSizeOverride = 'true';

    //***************************************************************//
    // This is a generic function that loads ADS.
    // *************************************************************** //
    (function () {
        oas_tag.version = '1';
        oas_tag.loadAd = oas_tag.loadAd || function(){};
        var oas = document.createElement("script"),
            protocol = "https:" == document.location.protocol ? "https://" : "http://",
            node = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
        
        oas.type = "text/javascript"; oas.async = true;
        
        oas.src = protocol + oas_tag.url + "/om/" + oas_tag.version + ".js";
        
        node.parentNode.insertBefore(oas, node);
    })();

    //***************************************************************//
    // The interval is injected from Journal level configuration setting.
    //***************************************************************//
   
    if(bannerUpdateInterval > 0)
    {
        window.setCustomInterval(function () {
            oas_tag.reloadAds();
        }, bannerUpdateInterval, bannerRefreshTime);
    }
    function setCustomInterval(callback, delay, repetitions) 
    {
        if(repetitions>0)
        {
            var x = 0;
            var intervalID = window.setInterval(function () {

                callback();

                if (++x === repetitions) {
                    window.clearInterval(intervalID);
                }
            }, delay);
        }
    }
  </script>
